 inamen se zyaadaatar siten muslim bahul ilaakon kii hi thim

 ) Preparations for the grand oath ceremony of the newly elected Prime Minister Narendra Modi and his Council of Ministers are almost complete
 is samaaroh ke liye kareeb 7000 logon ko nyotaa bheja gaya he
 The ceremony will be attended by veteran leaders of the country, many Chief Ministers and the heads of several countries, but West Bengal CM Mamata Banerjee has opted out of the ceremony
 bijepi (BJP) or trinmul congress (trinmool Congress) ke bich is maamle main vivaad shuru ho gaya he
 All Chief Ministers and leaders of major opposition parties have been invited
 karnataka ke mukhyamantri echdi kumaraswami, dilli ke siem arvind kejariwal isamen shaamil honge
 All the Chief Ministers of NDA are also reaching Delhi
 lekin bengal main bijepi ke 54 raajnneetik kaaryakartaaon kii hatya kaa aarope lagaae jane or sabake pariwaron ko shapath grahan main bulaane kii baat par mamata banerjee bhadak gayi or samaaroh main jane kaa iraadaa badal diya
 He says that there has been no political murder in Bengal
 unhone twit kiya, "shapath grahan loktantr ke samaaroh kaa pavitra avasar hota he

 yah kadam bharat ke pados main ek nai samrik ranneeti kii taraf ishaara karata he
 Foreign policy in which economic issues will be given more importance
 saal 2014 main piem modi ne pakistan ke tatkaaleen piem nawaz sharif samet sabhi saarc deshon ke rashtradhyakshon ko aamantrit kiya tha
 The fourth quarter results and inflation data for March for big companies like Infosys, TCS, Wipro, Reliance Industries will determine the direction of the stock market during the holiday week
 visheshgyon ne yah raay vyakt kii he
 The markets will remain closed on Ambedkar Jayanti on Monday and Good Friday on Friday
 bazaar sutron ne kaha ki share bazaar ke liye mahatvapurn utprerak companiyon ke march timahi or uske saath hi salanaa parinaam honge, jisaki shuruyaat mangalvaar ko pramukh iti company infosis ke nateezon ke saath hogi
 The results of companies such as TCS, Wipro, Glaxo smithkline Pharmaceuticals, HCL Technologies and Reliance Industries are to be announced this week, which will prove to be the catalyst for the market
 vyapak aarthik morche par thokabikri mulya suchakank (dablyoopiai) or upabhokta mulya suchakank (sipiai) aadhaarit mudrasphiti kaa aankada mangalvaar ko ghoshit kiya jayega
 Apart from all this, the stock market is awaiting the results of the Lok Sabha elections
 loksabhaa chunaavon ke liye matdaan 7 april se shuru ho chukaa he or yah 12 may tak chalegaa

 bonanja portpholio limited kii varisht shodh vishleshak nidhi saraswat ne kaha, is saptaah bazaar ke aage ke rukh ke liye mudrasphiti or infosis ke chauthi timahi ke parinaam nirnaayak tatv sabit honge
 The level of 6,800 points is a very important decisive level for the Nifty for the foreseeable future in the coming seasons and further buying above this level is likely to increase
 bazaar vishleshkon ne kaha ki videshi sansthagat niveshkon dwaara nivesh ke rakh, vaishvik sanket or dollar ke mukaable rupee kaa utaar-chadhaav bazaar ke rukh par asar daalate rahenge

 is sthiti ko dekhte hue bazaar main satarkta barte jane kii sambhaavna he
